Among the representatives are German Propaganda Minister Goebbels and Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss. Czech Foreign Minister Benes, Yugoslav Foreign Minister Yevtich, and Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu are holding a meeting of the Little Entente countries in Silesia, Romania, and were unable to attend the League of Nations Assembly. In the French delegation's seating area are Foreign Minister Pongou, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee Bérenger, and Hubert Delbos. (Havas dispatch)

Opening Speech 45

(Geneva) Norwegian Prime Minister Mowinckel, Chairman of the League of Nations Council, made a clear and straightforward statement on the World Economic Conference and the Disarmament Conference at the opening of the Assembly today, saying that both conferences were comparative failures. The reasons for this may be explained: it is difficult to gather many countries and have them unanimously agree and reach an agreement. A new dawn may be discovered, and a solid foundation for resolution may be found, but in reality, the results have not yet been achieved. The reason for this is that a basis for cooperation between countries with strong forces has not been established beforehand. If such powerful countries do not agree, satisfactory results cannot be obtained, as evidenced by the dispute over stabilizing currency prices at the Economic Conference. This statement can also be applied to the Disarmament Conference. The failure of the Disarmament Conference has led to the question of whether the League of Nations' prestige is more harmed than benefited if the Disarmament Conference ends abruptly without achieving anything.

Referring to the Far East, the Chairman also spoke of the dispute in the Far East, saying that although the League of Nations has made sincere efforts many times, it has ultimately failed to create a better situation. This fact has certainly not solidified the League of Nations' position in the eyes of the world, and will evoke feelings even worse than those produced by the situation in Europe. Fifteen years after the war, we feel that the progress towards seeking better understanding, a clearer atmosphere, and a more stable mentality among the peoples of all countries is still extremely small. This is our shame. Not only is progress extremely slow, but the idea of the possibility of war often lingers in our minds, permeating all countries, and is regarded as a major future problem. The League of Nations was once a group in which the world placed great hope. Now, the world blames the League of Nations, which is not only inevitable, but also reasonable. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Election of Chairman The Assembly then elected a chairman. The result of the vote was unexpected. South African representative Walter won with 30 votes out of 53, while the previously expected Mexican representative Najera received only 20 votes. It is now known that the British overseas territories and the Scandinavian countries began to campaign for the South African representative at the last minute, resulting in the above results. Walter has repeatedly given speeches in recent months attacking Japan's interference in Northeast affairs, which has made him famous. After Mr. Walter was elected, he took the chairmanship seat and thanked the representatives of all countries, declaring that he would treat everyone with fairness.

Adoption of the Agenda The Assembly then adjourned briefly and reconvened, adopting the agenda and deciding to establish five committees, which were instructed to meet separately in the afternoon and elect their respective chairmen. The Assembly itself is scheduled to reconvene at 5:30 PM to elect vice-chairmen. (Havas dispatch)

Seating Arrangement 46

(Geneva) The seating arrangement of each representative in the venue is arranged according to the French alphabet. Therefore, the representatives of the German and Austrian governments, who are currently in opposite positions, happen to be seated side by side in the first row. German Chief Representative Goebbels did not arrive until the last minute before the meeting began. Six men in plain clothes were guarding him. German journalists and onlookers welcomed him and gave the Fascist salute.

Reconvenes in the Afternoon After electing the chairman at this morning's meeting, the meeting adjourned at 1:20 PM and will reconvene at 5:00 PM this afternoon. It is expected that non-permanent directors will be elected at that time to replace Ireland, Guatemala, and Norway, whose terms have expired. (National News Agency dispatch) Behind-the-Scenes Negotiations The agenda of this session of the Assembly is unusually bland, with no major issues. The general debate of the representatives in the first week will likely reiterate dissatisfaction with last year's achievements and suggest ways to save the League of Nations from destruction. The most important developments during the session often do not occur in the Assembly hall, but in the lounges and hotels, where the representatives often make startling proposals during private discussions on the League of Nations and major European issues. (National News Agency dispatch)

The Jewish Question Given today's situation, it seems that the German treatment of the Jewish people will cause fierce debate in the Assembly. The Czech Republic and Poland attempted this spring to force the League of Nations Assembly to discuss the universal application of minority treaties, so that German Jews would receive the same treatment as Aryan Germans. Now, Jews everywhere have petitioned the League of Nations to intervene in Germany's rejection of Jews. If legal persons from countries allied with the League want to add fuel to the fire, it can turn into an extremely fierce debate. However, given the current situation in the Assembly, it seems that only this matter is enough to make the atmosphere tense. (National News Agency dispatch)

Red Flames Blaze High in Cuba, US Marines Land 50

Concerns about Armed Intervention Remain, Fearing Interference with Success of Pan-American Conference

Havana US Marines have landed in Santiago de Cuba. This is the first time US Marines have landed since the Cuban revolution began. Colonel Hernandez, the rebel leader from Morón, has arrived here and intends to visit President San Martín. According to Hernandez, he has never opposed the president. According to reports, after Hernandez's son was captured by government forces, he confessed to persuading his father to surrender. (Havas Telegram, 25th)

(Washington) A US government official stated today that communists trained in Moscow have established communist organizations throughout Cuba. Reports of armed communists in several locations in Cuba confiscating food without compensation are increasing anxiety in Washington political circles. There are increasing concerns that the unrest will intensify, making it necessary for the United States to send troops to land. Commanders of US warships stationed off the coast of Cuba have received instructions to deploy sailors ashore if necessary. At the same time, in diplomatic circles, it is believed that US intervention may hinder the success of the Pan-American Conference. This conference will be held in December in the capital of Uruguay. It is reported that President Roosevelt hopes to establish a closer diplomatic and commercial relationship between the United States and the Latin American republics at this conference to compensate for the United States' loss of trade with Europe. Diplomatic circles also believe that Japan will compare the United States' intervention in Cuba to Japan's invasion of Manchuria. Regarding the situation in Cuba, it is important to note that the Platt Amendment, which states [the United States should return the governing power of the island of Cuba to its people], also includes the following provisions: (1) Cuba shall never enter into any treaty that could impair its independence or allow any foreign power to station troops there. (2) Public debt should be limited to regular income. (3) Cuba shall permit the United States to intervene to preserve Cuba's independence and maintain a government sufficient to protect life, property, and individual liberty, and to fulfill the obligations of the Cuban government under the Treaty of Paris. (4) All actions taken during the US military occupation shall be deemed valid, and the rights obtained thereby shall be recognized. (5) Sanitation plans for Cuba's cities must be implemented to prevent the recurrence of epidemics and protect commerce. (6) The Isle of Pines is not within the territory of the Cuban Constitution. Ownership of the Isle of Pines will be determined by treaty in the future. (7) To enable the United States to maintain Cuba's independence, land needed for establishing naval stations may be sold or leased, as agreed upon with the Cuban President. (8) The above clauses must be included in the treaties concluded between Cuba and the United States. (Reuters Telegram, 24th)

Austrian Restoration Movement Revives 51

Archduke Otto Openly Demands the Throne and Vigorously Attacks National Socialism

Vienna Archduke Otto, son of the late Austrian Emperor Charles, publicly demanded the throne today while accepting honorary citizenship from three Austrian cities, indicating that the Austrian monarchist movement has openly commenced. The three cities are Hainfeld, Mürzzuschlag, and Judenburg, and their county executives presented the honorary citizenship to the Archduke here today. The Archduke, who is currently nineteen years old and residing in Switzerland, sent a representative to accept the honor, accompanied by a handwritten letter guaranteeing that with God's blessing, the time for him to lead Austria again is not far off. He believes that the laws restricting the activities of the Habsburg royal family will soon be repealed. Without these unfair laws, he will occupy the position that the people desire and that his duty requires. Finally, he declared that the methods of National Socialism are not suitable for Austria and that accepting them blindly would be tantamount to treason. Since Dollfuss formed the new cabinet last week, monarchists in Austria have been celebrating, believing that the time for restoration is drawing near, and the possibility of restoration is now being openly discussed by the people. (National Telegram, 24th)

White House Financial Conference 52

Government Plans to Exert All Efforts to Release Frozen Loans, Large-Scale Encouragement Campaign to Begin Next Month

Reuters, Washington, 25th The White House held an important conference last night to discuss financial matters. Afterward, the President's Secretary stated that the purpose of the meeting was to study the current financial situation, with particular attention to making credit available to industry and commerce, but there was no intention to immediately adopt new inflationary measures. It is generally believed that this statement indicates that, in any event, there will likely be no direct currency inflation measures taken in the near future, and it indicates that the government will make every effort to circulate the stagnant deposits of closed or restricted banks. It is reported that the discussion at the meeting focused on the difficult problem of releasing these stagnant deposits. Secretary of Agriculture Wallace stated today that if Americans do not want to adopt a world trade policy suitable for creditors, then the United States must eliminate the production of 400,000 acres of excess farmland that were cultivated before the war. He believes that managing production is essential.

Reuters, Washington, 25th General Johnson, the administrator of the Recovery Act, plans to launch a large-scale campaign on October 1st to encourage people to buy promptly in order to stimulate the circulation of money. The government's new plan seeks to coordinate the efforts of four government agencies to release stagnant deposits and place banks on a sound footing. The Financial Rehabilitation Society will purchase preferred securities to activate bank capital. The Agricultural Loan Bureau and the Domestic Loan Office will repay mortgage assets with immediately saleable bonds (in effect, guaranteeing mortgages). The Mortgage Guarantee Society will guarantee the deposits of new depositors.

Holy Shroud Open for Viewing 54

National, Turin, 25th The shroud in which Jesus's body was wrapped after being taken down from the cross, known as the Holy Shroud by Christians, is the most precious relic in the religion. After being transported from the East to Europe, it was treasured by the royal families of France and Austria. Two hundred years ago, it came into the hands of the Italian House of Savoy, where it has been carefully stored in the cathedral here. A separate chapel has been built to house it. After the Italian princess married the Belgian prince in 1930, it was opened for viewing once. This year marks the 1,900th anniversary of Jesus's ascension, and it was opened for public viewing starting today, scheduled to last until October 15th. When the public viewing ceremony was held today, all the princes and princesses of the House of Savoy currently residing in Italy personally attended the church. All the civil and military officials of the city participated devoutly. The grandeur and solemnity of the ceremony were unparalleled.

Central and National Government Memorial Week Reports 56

Li Yuying: Reviving Agriculture; Sun Ke: The Principle of People's Livelihood

(Nanjing) The Central Government held its 97th Memorial Week at 8 AM on the 25th. Attendees included Central Committee members Li Ciwen, Li Yuying, Chu Minyi, Wang Qi, Zheng Zhan'nan, Xiao Zhongzhen, Chen Lifu, Li Jingzhai, Li Zonghuang, Miao Peicheng, Ma Chaojun, and all staff members, totaling 500 people. Chu Minyi chaired the meeting, and Li Yuying gave a report, stating that China is an agricultural country, so agricultural issues are very important. The Premier's teachings are full of instructions on revitalizing agriculture and reviving rural areas. At present, rural areas are already bankrupt, and solving this problem is the top priority. Recently, the people of the country have also paid attention to this, and there have been designs, research associations, or discussion groups on reviving rural areas, or the establishment of various experimental villages. There are already more than 30 such places across the country. Regarding rural relief, it should involve projects such as water conservancy, land reclamation, and industry. To make rural areas sound, it should involve rural autonomy, self-defense, education, and economics. This year, when Mr. Zhang Jingjiang and I attended the Zouping Rural Discussion Conference, we carefully studied the issue and felt that increasing agricultural production is the foundation of rural relief. If production is not increased, and only the education and living standards of farmers are raised, their desires will increase, their production power will decrease, and farmers will have a tendency to take off their short shirts and put on long shirts. Therefore, my conclusions are: (1) Follow the Premier's teachings and focus on agriculture. (2) Reviving rural areas should start with increasing agricultural production. (3) Focus on practical work and do not engage in empty talk. The meeting adjourned at 9 AM. (Central News Agency Telegram, 25th)

(Nanjing) The National Government held its Memorial Week at 8 AM on the 25th. Regulations on the Use of Police Equipment 62

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 25th, promulgating the Regulations on the Use of Police Equipment. The full text of the order and the Regulations on the Use of Police Equipment are as follows: Article 1: The police equipment used by police officers and policemen when performing their duties shall be batons, knives, and guns. Article 2: Police officers and policemen may use batons for directing traffic or suppressing disturbances when performing their duties, when deemed necessary. Article 3: Police officers and policemen shall not use knives or guns when performing their duties unless one of the following circumstances exists: (1) The life or body of a police officer or policeman is threatened and must be defended with a knife or gun to resist or defend themselves. (2) The land, buildings, or the life, body, or property of a person being defended by a police officer or policeman is threatened, and a knife or gun must be used to protect them. (3) A wanted criminal escapes or resists arrest, and there is no other way to stop them except by using a knife or gun. (4) Rioters disturb public order, and a knife or gun must be used to suppress them. Article 4: When police officers and policemen are about to use knives or guns, they shall provide a warning first, unless the situation is extremely urgent. Article 5: Police officers and policemen shall immediately cease using police equipment when those involved show signs of submission. Article 6: Police officers and policemen shall take care not to injure other persons when using police equipment. Article 7: Police officers and policemen shall take care not to injure the vital parts of a person's body when using police equipment, unless the situation is extremely urgent. Article 8: Police officers and policemen shall immediately report the circumstances to their superiors after using batons, regardless of whether anyone is injured or not. Article 9: Those who use knives or guns without one of the circumstances specified in Article 3 shall be disciplined by their superiors. If anyone is injured or killed as a result, in addition to the state providing medical expenses or compensation to the victim, the offending police officer or policeman shall be punished in accordance with the criminal law. Article 10: These regulations shall apply to military police when performing police duties. Article 11: These regulations shall take effect on the date of promulgation. (Central News Agency Telegram, 25th)

Page 9

Collected Land Tax Surcharges in Installments and Averaged

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance, in order to consolidate land tax surcharges, consulted with various ministries and commissions to formulate measures, which were submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and circulated for compliance. Currently, the amount of land tax surcharges collected in each installment in various localities is inconsistent. Generally, the amount of surcharges in the first installment is much higher than in other installments. Even most of the surcharges are collected under the first installment of land tax. At that time, farmers have no large-scale harvest, and ordering them to pay huge amounts of taxes is not in line with the principle of measuring taxpaying ability when collecting taxes. Moreover, farmers' capital is attached to the harvest. In the past, when farmers were farming and irrigating, they urgently needed funds, and collecting more than half of the annual land tax surcharge caused a shortage of funds for production, which had a significant impact on agricultural production and farmers' economy. It is a universally recognized principle that taxes should be collected at the most convenient time. Now, collecting huge amounts of taxes during the busy farming season is completely contrary to this principle. At a time when the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, and the central and local governments are jointly seeking relief, land tax surcharges should be corrected as soon as possible and collected in installments within the prescribed limits. If the land tax was originally collected in two installments, each installment should collect half of the surcharges. If it was previously collected in three installments, each installment should collect one-third of the surcharges. The timing of collection should not violate agriculture. This is a point that requires special attention in consolidating land tax surcharges, and it is also closely related to rural revitalization. Yesterday, a special instruction was given to the finance departments and bureaus of each province and city to instruct the counties to comply and report the handling situation to the ministry for inspection. (Special Telegram, 25th)

Chen performed aerial acrobatics, including sideslips, low-altitude flights, ascending turns, and letting go of the controls, which were met with thunderous applause from the crowd. After the performance, Chen gave a speech, encouraging the people of Xuzhou to nationalize aviation and make aviation a national cause. Then, at 2:40 PM, he boarded the plane with Pan Dingxin, who had come with him, and headed north towards Jin amid cheers. (25th Dispatch)

(Jinan) At 4:30 PM, Chen Wenlin and Pan Dingxin flew to Jinan, circling the city three times. They first landed at Xinzhuang training ground, then took off again and landed at Zhangzhuang airfield. They took a car to the YMCA to rest. According to them, the flight between Xu and Jin took two hours, flying at 4,000 meters and passing over Mount Tai. The purpose of the flight is threefold: First, to promote aviation to save the country and the self-made aircraft; second, to test the long-distance flight capability of the first self-made aircraft; and third, to observe the terrain, air routes, and climate of our country to prepare for the development of aviation. They are scheduled to fly to Tianjin tomorrow afternoon, then to Ping, Baoding, Shijiazhuang, Zhangde, Zhengzhou, Zhumadian, Hankou, Jiujiang, Anqing, and Nanjing, which will take twelve days, and then return to Xiamen via Shanghai, Hangzhou, Wenzhou, and Fuzhou. (25th Dispatch)

Arrangement of Chen Jiongming's Funeral Hall 88

(Hong Kong) Chen Jiongming's spiritual hall is decorated with the Five-Colored Flag, flanked by red, yellow, and blue flags with blue lines at the end of the flags, marked with a well character in the center. According to Chen Yansheng, a confidant of Chen, the Five-Colored Flag was the national flag that Chen had supported throughout his life, and the flags on both sides are the flags of the Zhi Gong Party. The "well" character represents "farmers owning their land." Chen was the leader of the Zhi Gong Party, so the party flag should be hung after his death to show respect. The blue cloth on the coffin is a sign of anti-filial piety because Chen still has a 13-year-old mother. In short, the layout of the spiritual hall is strange and colorful, and indescribable. Only Chen Mingshu and Weng Guiqing came to offer condolences on the 24th. (25th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Zhejiang Martial Law Headquarters Closed 92

(Hangzhou) The Zhejiang Provincial Capital Martial Law Headquarters has been ordered by the military to close. Japanese Army Warns Fang's Troops to Withdraw from War Zone by Deadline 93

Japanese Troops Planned to Invade Beiping, Japanese Military Planned to Send Eighth Division to Drive Out Fang's Troops

Our Side Refused Japanese Troops to Enter War Zone, Japanese Planes Flew Over Ping, Dispersing Warning Leaflets

Beiping Special Dispatch, Fang Zhenwu's troops suddenly entered the war zone of Huairou County from the Chahar-Rehe border on the 20th, a bolt from the blue, shocking all parties. The authorities have been negotiating with the Japanese side to find a solution to prevent future troubles. The Kwantung Army Headquarters issued a warning, limiting Fang's troops to completely withdraw from the war zone by the 26th. Details are recorded below:

Fang's Troops Fled into War Zone 94

Fang Zhenwu, after meeting in Dushikou with representatives of Ji Hongchang, Zheng Guilin, and Tang Yulin, Liu Guitang, Li Shouxin, etc., decided to change their flags and jointly organize, left Dushikou and fled east, detouring through the Fengning County territory on the Rehe border, and entered the war zone, invading the Great Wall through Changyuankou. On the morning of the 20th, the vanguard of four to five hundred cavalry arrived in Huairou County. The security team in the city only had one hundred and twenty people, with weak strength. Furthermore, they had only recently arrived in Huairou to garrison, and the people's hearts were not attached. Fang's troops went straight to the city, the security team closed the city gate, preparing to defend. Local gentry and merchants, fearing that the area would be devastated if Fang's troops attacked if the city was not opened, asked the county magistrate Xu Wenquan and the security team leader to open the city to welcome the enemy. Fang's troops then occupied the county seat.

Attempt to Invade Beiping 95

After Fang's troops' vanguard cavalry entered the city, the remaining troops arrived one after another. Fang himself also entered the city on the 21st, setting up a headquarters in a certain prison shop in the city, with the banner "Punish XX Allied Army". Fang's troops who arrived in Huairou include one guard battalion with more than one hundred and fifty men, one cavalry division with more than eight hundred men, and three infantry brigades with more than one thousand two hundred men. In addition, there are attached training corps. Although the organization is extremely large, there are only two thousand people. Less than two-thirds of the troops have firearms, and most of them are pistols. The strength is extremely weak. The guard battalion is currently stationed in the city, and the cavalry and training corps are stationed in Jiao Xiaocun. The infantry is stationed in Diaoyutai and Shichang villages. There are about six to seven hundred plainclothes soldiers inside and outside Huairou City. When Fang's troops first entered the city, they set up outposts to defend and cut off traffic, allowing people to leave but not enter. From Huairou to the south, sentries were placed in Qiaozicun and Nanshicao in the sixth district of Shunyi County, extorting supplies and cash from merchants and residents. A support bureau was established in the city to handle military affairs. Slogans were posted all over the streets and important places, mostly with the meaning of defending the local area and resisting the central government. After arriving in Huairou on the 21st, Fang convened a military-civilian conference. Fang and his entourage all gave speeches in public and distributed many leaflets. After the military-civilian conference, military conferences were held continuously to discuss the plan to flee and disturb the area. According to reports, their first step was to invade Beiping. Fang's troops would go south from Huairou, and Ji Hongchang, Liu Guitang, Tang Yulin, and Zheng Guilin's troops would go south from the Nankou area. The second step, if the attack on Beiping failed, would be to turn to Luandong and join forces with the bandits in Luandong to make a major move. After deliberation, it was decided that after Ji, Liu, Tang, Zheng, and other troops arrived, they would begin their first step of the plan. At the same time, they would also establish contact with Luandong.

Japanese Limit Fang's Troops to Withdraw 96

On the 21st, two Japanese military vehicles carrying forty to fifty Japanese soldiers and three or four officers, carrying two machine guns, arrived at the east gate of Huairou from Miyun and spread out, preparing to shoot. Then, one Japanese officer entered the city and went straight to Fang's headquarters, holding talks with Fang's troops for a long time. The content is unknown. After the talks, Fang sent personnel to escort him out of the city, and he led the soldiers back north in the original military vehicles. At the same time, a Japanese plane came to Huairou and Shunyi to scout. After our side made representations, the Japanese side issued a warning to Fang's troops, limiting them to withdraw from the war zone by the 26th. In the past few days, Fang's troops have been extensively extorting from merchants and residents in Huairou. The supplies and other items obtained have been loaded onto large carts and moved outside the city, appearing to be fleeing elsewhere. It is said that Fang, with limited strength, does not dare to flee south and may flee to Luandong to join the bandits and seek a major move.

Authorities' Countermeasures 97

After receiving the report that Fang's troops had fled into the war zone, the authorities immediately convened military, political, and diplomatic officials to study countermeasures. All agreed that Huairou is close to Beiping and is located in the war zone. Sending troops to suppress them would require the consent of the Japanese side. After discussion, it was decided: (1) According to the agreement made at the time of the ceasefire agreement, our side could send troops to the war zone to suppress bandits when necessary with the understanding of the Japanese side, make representations to the Japanese side and seek the consent of the Japanese side to send troops to suppress them in order to avoid future troubles. (2) Because Huairou is close to Beiping and Changping and other places, make necessary arrangements at the connection points to prevent Fang's troops from fleeing and disturbing the area.

Situation of Negotiations with Japan 98

After the authorities decided on the countermeasures, they made the necessary arrangements while sending Yin Tong and Liu Shisun to negotiate with the Japanese side. Yin and others visited military attache Chiba at the Japanese embassy on the previous day (21st), explaining our side's intentions and seeking the Japanese side's consent for our side to send troops to suppress them to avoid future troubles. Chiba telegraphed the Kwantung Army to ask for instructions. Yesterday (22nd) at 5:00 PM, Chiba visited He Yingqin at Jurentang, saying that he had received a reply from the Kwantung Army. In order to maintain the spirit of the ceasefire agreement, it was decided to issue a serious warning to Fang Zhenwu, limiting him to withdraw from the war zone by the 26th, otherwise drastic measures would be taken. He also declared that the Kwantung Army believed that Fang's troops had communist elements and planned to send a part of the Eighth Division into the Great Wall to suppress Fang's troops. The reason he gave was that the Japanese army had new-style weapons such as airplanes and tanks, which would facilitate the rapid elimination of Fang's troops. The authorities, considering that the war zone is our country's territory, and suppressing Fang's troops did not require the Japanese side to act on their behalf, rejected it based on the agreement and put forward three reasons: (1) If the Japanese army that had already withdrawn according to the agreement were to re-enter the war zone, countries around the world would definitely become suspicious of Japan, and it would also increase the difficulties for both sides when Japanese soldiers later returned. (2) If the Japanese army entered the war zone to drive out Fang's troops in order to quickly suppress them, using airplanes to bomb and artillery to bombard, the innocent people in the war-torn Huairou area would inevitably be affected, which would not be conducive to taking care of the local area. (3) Fang's troops are weak and will not flee south. If they are helpless, they will inevitably flee to various parts of the war zone. If the Japanese army tracks and pursues them, the entire war zone will inevitably be devastated. It is hoped that the Japanese side will follow the spirit of the agreement and let our side send troops to suppress them alone. Chiba promised to consider it and telegraphed Tokyo and Changchun for instructions. Our side is currently waiting for the Japanese side to reply before determining the policy.

Japanese Planes Suddenly Fly Over Ping 99

While negotiations between our side and the Japanese army to resolve the Fang troops had not yet been settled, Japanese planes suddenly flew over Ping and distributed police leaflets. This morning (23rd), a Japanese plane took off from Miyun and flew south along Huairou, Niulanshan, Shunyi, and Gaoliying to Ping. At 10:20 AM, it was discovered over Andingmen and flew south along Dongsi Pailou, distributing leaflets along the way. The flight was extremely low, and the sound shook the roofs, causing panic among the citizens. When it flew to the Japanese barracks in Dongjiaomin Lane, it dropped a communication tube and circled once over the city of Ping before flying north. The original text of the leaflet that was distributed is recorded below: "Warning to Fang Zhenwu and the armies allied with him, on May 31, Showa 8 (1933), the Kwantung Army and the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Committee of the National Government negotiated a ceasefire. At that time, both sides agreed and signed that the Chinese army must not advance to the area north of the line connecting Yanqing, Changping, Gaoliying, Shunyi, Tongzhou, Xianghe, Baodi, Lintingzhen, Ninghe, and Lutai. However, the allied army commanded by the current Army Commander Fang Zhenwu is active in the area north of that line. The Kwantung Army will absolutely not tolerate this action no matter what the reason. Army Commander Fang must immediately begin to withdraw to the area south of the agreed line and completely withdraw by the evening of the 26th. After the 27th, not a single soldier is allowed to remain. This is a strict requirement. If the withdrawal is not fully implemented by the deadline, the Kwantung Army will immediately send troops to suppress it decisively. Declaration, September 22, Showa 8 (1933), Commander of the Great Japanese Army."

He Yingqin's Talk 100

He Yingqin told reporters this morning that Fang Zhenwu's actions had gone beyond the norm. Tang Yulin, Ji Hongchang, Liu Guitang, and others had reportedly not participated. Fang's mask had been torn off, and Tang and others would not willingly support him as their leader. There are suspicious points in Fang's troops gaining passage through Rehe territory to flee into the war zone. However, the Japanese side yesterday made every effort to express that there were communist elements mixed in Fang's and Ji's troops, and the Japanese side was determined to expel them and would absolutely not allow them to stay in the war zone. From this point of view, Fang's troops would not be difficult to resolve, and the overall situation in North China would not be affected. In Huairou, Fang's troops only had Wang Zhongfu's troops of more than two thousand people, with only six to seven hundred guns, a weak force. After obtaining the Japanese side's consent, sending troops to suppress them would be very easy to eliminate. Negotiations are currently underway with the Japanese side. Fang originally had a considerable position, and for the sake of settling matters peacefully, a considerable margin is still being left for him to open a path to self-renewal. As for the small number of bandits of "Old Rat" who fled to Sanhe County, there seems to be no connection with Fang, but because they are more than a hundred miles apart, it is easier to collude. Currently, all the diplomatic and aftermath matters in North China are pending. All parties are eagerly awaiting the return of Chairman Huang (Fu) to the north, and I have also telegraphed him to urge him. I received a reply yesterday, saying that he would go north after completing the "two incidents." Everything will be easier to handle after Chairman Huang arrives. (23rd) Da Songjiang

Inhuman Slave Abuse Case 101

A man surnamed Gao from Xiatang, Bencheng County, works at a bank in Shanghai. His concubine lives in Songjiang. Two years ago, they bought a girl, initially as an adopted daughter, but later changed her status to a slave. The slave girl is eight years old. For some unknown reason, she was abused by the concubine, with her whole body covered in wounds. The fingertips of both hands were burned and scalded, with obvious burn holes at the fingertips. The most unbearable thing was that she was forced to eat her own excrement. If she disobeyed slightly, she would be severely beaten. The matter was heard by a neighbor surnamed Zhang, who tried to rescue her from the fire pit and asked someone to discuss with the Gao family about letting the girl be adopted, slightly compensating for the cost of food and clothing spent over the years. They have already taken her back to raise her. Thus, this cruel and inhumane abuse has gradually spread. According to the case of Jiang Wang's abuse of her adopted daughter Tangying, which was reported by the hall directors, the court has already punished her.

Suzhou

[P Retrial of Suqian County Magistrate's Case]

Suqian County Magistrate Cui Qingshan embezzled public funds and acted illegally, which was reported by someone. The Civil Affairs Department sent Cui to the Jiangsu Higher Court. The first instance sentenced him to two years in prison and fined him 1,000 yuan. Cui refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the Supreme Court, which sent the case back for retrial. The retrial has been concluded, and the verdict was pronounced yesterday (25th), sentencing him to one year and four months in prison and fining him 600 yuan. Cui still expressed his dissatisfaction and planned to file an appeal, requesting to suspend the detention in court. The presiding judge agreed to wait for a ruling.

Narcotics Investigation Office Ordered to Close

There was a rumor a month ago that the Wuxian County Narcotics Investigation Office would be abolished and reorganized into a Tobacco Prohibition Bureau, but it did not materialize. It is now learned that the office received an order from the province yesterday (25th) to close immediately.

Wuxi

Nephew Beats Uncle to Death After Drinking 102

Qin Heduo, a villager in the Qin Gengshang area of the 442nd Tu, about a mile away from Anzhen in the eighth district of the county, was 54 years old. His wife, Ni, was about the same age. On the evening of the 28th day of the seventh month, after Ah Duo had dinner, he suddenly had a quarrel with his nephew He Sanmei about the redemption of the house. At that time, both sides had drunk a little wine with dinner and were slightly drunk. In a moment of passion, they fought each other. Ah Duo was old and weak and was knocked to the ground by Ah San. His right waist happened to hit the threshold of the back door of Mei Gen's house. It was heard that Ah San also pressed on Ah Duo, causing Ah Duo's waist to be injured, his breath faint, and his breathing unceasing. Afterwards, he was bedridden and in extreme pain. He died of exhaustion the day before yesterday afternoon. The 16th Public Security Bureau of the jurisdiction sent police to detain and arrest the murderers Qin Ah San and Qin Meigen for questioning. The Tu Zheng Qin Fengming (the deceased's brother) was ordered to report to the county court yesterday with the deceased's wife, Ni. The investigating prosecutor held a hearing, and Tu Zheng provided the same information. The deceased's wife requested to waive the autopsy, but the judge refused and ordered them to return. It was decided that the police officers would take the Changshu small wheel to the village for the autopsy at 7 am today to verify the case.

Yinjiang

Setting Up Warehouses to Aid Rural Economy 103

The local party and government organs, in order to aid the rural economy, commissioned Xue Chan and Sun Ren, the district chief of the 11th district, to go to Shanghai to discuss with Zou Bingwen, director of the rural loan department of the Shanghai Bank, to set up a warehouse at the original site of Qingyang Town's Junda Hall, modeled after the Xiaoxian method. Both parties negotiated and agreed to establish it, trying it out for one year, with the opening scheduled for October 15th, starting with agricultural warehouses and commodity storage and mortgage, promoting various production cooperative enterprises, and aiming to revitalize the countryside. If the local environment does not create problems, the cotton cooperative in Shazhou can be established first.

Zhenjiang

Male Corpse Found Murdered in Park 104

Yesterday at about 3:00 PM, a grass-picking woman in the Boxian Park, on a small path halfway up the mountain that leads to the small wharf, saw a pile of messy grass ahead and immediately went forward to pick it up. Unexpectedly, as soon as she brushed the grass aside, a corpse suddenly appeared before her eyes. The woman was shocked and screamed wildly. The incident was heard by the park office, which immediately ordered the local baojia to report to the court for an autopsy and notified the local public security bureau to send personnel for inspection. The deceased was about twenty years old, with a small, thin build and his face facing the ground. He was wearing a gray-striped spring gown, striped pongee trousers, and square-toed black silk shoes, looking like a small businessman. A black artificial silk trouser belt was wrapped around his neck several times, presumably causing his death.

製綫業工人停業 105

The entire body of workers in the thread-making industry of Zhenjiang, including Li Jinyong, etc., previously, because the capital side of the industry began implementing a 30% reduction in wages on the 19th of this month, the labor side, in order to avoid disputes, continued to work for three days. On the one hand, they requested the capital side to maintain the original wage rate, and on the other hand, they submitted a petition to the party and government organs requesting mediation, and also expressed their grievances. They stated that even at the original wage rate, they felt that their lives were still difficult, and if it were changed to a 30% reduction, the danger to their lives would be even more precarious, etc. Subsequently, because the capital side did not provide a satisfactory response, the labor side temporarily went on strike yesterday, awaiting the party and government organs to send personnel to mediate, it is said.

Yangzhou

Northwest Two Townships Report Disaster 106

Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been little rainfall in the four townships. The highland fields in the northwest two townships have suffered from drought, resulting in no harvest. The villagers in the area have reported to the district head in charge, who has forwarded the reports to the county government for disaster relief. They have also requested that personnel be sent to conduct a re-inspection. County Magistrate Ma, upon receiving the report, intends to personally inspect the area as a basis for submitting a report to the provincial government to request exemption from land taxes.

Taichang Steamship Company Adds Siyang Route 107

The Taichang Steamship Company, in order to facilitate passengers between Yang (Yangzhou) and Si (Siyuangou), has specially added a Siyang route. It departs from Si at 7:00 AM every day and from Yang at 1:30 PM. It has already been reported to the Jiangdu and Yizheng county governments for record.

Nantong

Chen Maojie Arrives in Tongzhou to Inspect the Collapsed Dike 108

The Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee, considering the severe tidal disaster caused by the recent collapse of the Nantong river dike, with the riverbank collapsing more and more severely and Wolf Mountain gradually sinking into the river, causing the Yangtze River waterway to undergo

drastic changes, has specially dispatched committee member Chen Maojie to Tongzhou to inspect the collapsed dike and expedite the emergency rescue project.

Flood Victims in the Tidal Disaster Area Petition 109

The Wolf Mountain area suffered a severe tidal disaster, with more than ten breaches that have not yet been completely blocked. On the 24th, the tidal wave, taking advantage of the wind and rain, flooded in again. The water in each embankment was five to six feet deep. The disaster victims, supporting the old and carrying the young, rushed to the city to petition the county government and district office to quickly block the breaches and provide relief. The authorities agreed to do so, and the disaster victims left. A total of more than 2,000 households were affected by this disaster, with extremely heavy losses.

Hangzhou

Tao Sijin and Xu Qinwen Sentenced for Endangering the Country 110

The case of Tao Sijin, a female student at the West Lake Art Academy, brutally killing her classmate Liu Mengying was remanded by the Supreme Court to the Higher Court for retrial. The judgment was that Tao Sijin was sentenced to life imprisonment and Xu Qinwen was acquitted. Tao has expressed her acceptance of the verdict. However, the prosecutor believes that the sentence is too lenient and has appealed to the Supreme Court again. Additionally, suspecting that Xu Qinwen and Tao Sijin have joined the Communist Party, a separate case was filed against Xu and Tao for endangering the Republic of China. The Higher Court concluded the trial, and yesterday (the 25th) at 10:00 AM, Judge Fu Guanhua of the Second Criminal Tribunal ordered the bailiffs to bring Tao from the military prison and detention center separately. Xu was in shackles, wearing a dark blue serge suit and black leather shoes. Tao wore a white short shirt and black skirt. Both were quite composed. After the judge questioned them about their age and origin, the judgment was announced: Xu Qinwen was acquitted of the charge of endangering the Republic of China by organizing a group, but knowing that Liu Mengying and others were communists, he continuously harbored and concealed them without reporting, and was sentenced to five years of imprisonment. Tao Sijin was acquitted of the charge of using writing for treasonous propaganda, but was sentenced to five years of imprisonment for the crime of endangering the Republic of China by organizing a group. The number of days in custody before the judgment is confirmed will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. If they do not agree, they can appeal within ten days. The judge then ordered Xu Qinwen and Tao Sijin to be taken back into custody.

Security Department Executes Notorious Bandit from Sheng County by Shooting 111

The Zhejiang Provincial Security Department, based on a confidential report that Zheng Bingquan, a notorious bandit from Sheng County, had fled to Shanghai, dispatched detectives to Shanghai to arrest him and bring him to justice. After questioning, it was confirmed that Zheng Bingquan was Chen Zhongxiao, also known as "Old Thin Knife." He confessed that in April of the lunar calendar last year, he had colluded with others to kidnap Xu Rongqing, the son of Xu Gengchan of Shanggang Village, and Lin Zhangsen of Changpan Village, extorting money and sharing the loot. He also admitted that he used the name Chen Zhongxiao to extort money from two unnamed families in Songjiadun, and then fled to the Shanghai Concession to hide. He denied other cases of murder, arson, and robbery, attributing them to other bandits. He admitted to the kidnapping and extortion of Xu Rongqing and the letter of intimidation. He was sentenced to death according to law. Yesterday (the 25th) at 8:00 AM, personnel were dispatched to the military prison to identify Zheng Bingquan, confirm his identity, and escort him to an open space outside Qingbo Gate for execution by shooting.

Local News

Song Ziwen Discusses Entrusting the Central Bank with the Sale of American Cotton 114

American Wheat Price Reduced Before Shipment

Economic Committee Reorganization Expected Next Week

Finances of North China Resolved, Song Not Traveling North for Now

Minister of Finance Song Ziwen, who arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing a few days ago to discuss important official matters and will return to Nanjing next week, met with reporters from various newspapers at his residence at 2:00 PM yesterday. He made the following statements on important issues such as the promotion of American cotton and wheat, the expansion of the Economic Committee, and the finances of North China.

Entrusting the Central Bank with the Sale of American Cotton 115

Song said, the first batch of American cotton will arrive in Shanghai soon, and subsequent batches will be shipped to China in succession. A plan for selling the cotton has been determined, which is to entrust the Central Bank to manage it, and other people will be hired to promote the sales and bear the economic responsibility. The cotton will be sold and the proceeds will be remitted immediately, not sold directly to manufacturers. Since this matter is commercial in nature, Japanese merchants are also not prohibited from purchasing it. The government and manufacturers will fully cooperate. Rumors that American cotton will be exempt from tariffs and sold at a reduced price are all false. In short, the government seeks to neither lose nor gain from the purchase and sale. The future selling price of cotton will depend on the domestic cotton production and the state of the yarn market. As for the high price of American wheat, he has requested the American side to reduce the price slightly, and there is a tendency to agree. The wheat has not yet been loaded on ships and will not arrive in China for several months.

Economic Committee Focuses on Talent 116

The National Economic Committee was originally headed by Mr. Chiang Kai-shek as chairman and me as vice chairman. It has now been decided to reorganize the committee, abolish the chairman system, and replace it with a standing committee consisting of the heads of the Executive Yuan and Legislative Yuan, as well as myself. The committee was established two years ago and usually focuses on practical work, without engaging in publicity. The expenses are also extremely economical. Mr. Chiang has always emphasized the use of technical talent in personnel matters, seeking people based on their skills and not assigning people to positions for which they are not qualified. The committee strives to recruit technical talent from all over the country to dedicate themselves to technical work and aims to detach itself from political relations. It is hoped that the committee organization can be maintained permanently and that the staff can serve with peace of mind. Furthermore, the future Cotton Industry Control Committee or other committees to be established by the Economic Committee will have more participation from people in society and less participation from government personnel. The central government will play a guiding and assisting role. As for the issue of technical cooperation with the League of Nations, people like Rajchman are purely in the position of guest advisors, assisting in the process, and the sovereignty over all facilities remains in our hands. Furthermore, the organizational regulations of the committee have been passed by the Legislative Yuan and were originally scheduled to be reorganized and established within the next few days. However, because I am busy in Shanghai this week and unable to leave, I must return to Nanjing next week, at which time it can be formally established.

Song Himself Will Not Travel North for Now 117

Regarding the financial problems of North China, before I went to Lushan, I had already discussed a solution with Huang Yingbai, the chairman of the Peiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee. The most important point now is to save all expenses. As the saying goes, "If you cannot increase revenue, then reduce expenses." The military expenses of North China have now been reduced to the amount during Zhang Hanqing's time in Peiping, which is 4.5 million yuan per month. The amount will be further reduced depending on the situation. In the future, the finances of North China will be directly handled by the Ministry of Finance to avoid any obstacles. As for the rumor that I will travel to North China with Chairman Huang (Fu) to thoroughly reorganize the finances of North China, I have never had such an intention. Currently, there are many affairs in Nanjing and Shanghai, and I cannot spare the time to go elsewhere. Furthermore, since there is already a plan for the finances of North China, there is no need for me to go north.

Imposing Tariffs on Foreign Rice Will Proceed Step by Step 118

Song then discussed the issue of imposing tariffs on imported foreign rice, saying that the imposition of rice tariffs is related to the livelihood of the people of the whole country and is not merely a matter of financial revenue. My opinion on this matter is that the first step is to eliminate the transit tax on domestic rice and at the same time order all provinces to abolish the rice permit tax and all other surtaxes, so that domestically produced rice can circulate freely within the country. This has already been implemented in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces. The second step is to impose a certain restriction on foreign rice, observing the rise and fall of rice prices at any time to verify the surplus or deficiency of domestic rice. If so, then the import of foreign rice can be taxed when it reaches a certain price, and exempted from tax when it exceeds this price. When I proposed this plan, the method was very suitable for regulating domestic food supply, but politicians spread rumors, saying that Guangdong Province relied entirely on rice from Siam and Saigon for maintenance, and that the government's proposal was a poisonous plan to make the people of Guangdong eat tribute rice. As a result, the government was unwilling to cause political disputes over the food issue and did not fully implement it, only discussing it separately with each province. Now that Guangdong has suddenly implemented the collection of foreign rice tax, it proves that the collection of foreign rice tax is necessary to regulate domestic food supply. Now that Guangdong has also felt this point, it is gradually maturing and the method can be fully implemented. As for foreign wheat and flour, the same will be done and will be discussed in detail in the Economic Committee.

Increasing Production in the Lianghuai Reclamation Area 119

I have submitted a proposal to the Executive Yuan for the reclamation of wasteland in the Lianghuai reclamation area. This matter originally belonged to the Ministry of Finance, but because it is related to various agencies, it will be transferred to the National Economic Committee for handling in the future. The motive for my proposal is entirely because the Lianghuai salt area occupies a very large area, and it is a pity to leave it barren. Therefore, we should find a way to have the government advance a huge amount of capital to plan for reclamation. After the budget plan is implemented, it can increase the people's production by 100 million yuan per year. Although it is not directly beneficial to the government, it is a matter of national economy and people's livelihood and should not be delayed, he said.

First Batch of American Cotton to Arrive 120

More Than 11,000 Bales to Arrive in Shanghai on the 29th

The first batch of cotton purchased by our country from the United States with borrowed funds has already been shipped and is on its way and is about to arrive in Shanghai. The details of the arrival and transit of the goods are reported as follows:

Exact Number of Cotton Bales 121

The total number of cotton bales purchased by our country from the United States with borrowed funds is more than 220,000. The first batch was shipped from New Orleans by the Dodwell & Co.'s S.S. "Asia Maru" on August 15th, via the Panama Canal to our country. The exact number of cotton bales loaded on the ship is 11,350. In addition to the cotton, the ship also carried a batch of kerosene for the Texaco Company, which was also shipped to Shanghai for unloading.

No Stopping in Japan 122

The ship was originally scheduled to stop at Kobe, Japan, for two days before coming to Shanghai. However, because the ship was eager to come to Shanghai, Dodwell & Co. telegraphed the shipowner, instructing the ship not to stop when passing through the East Sea and to proceed directly to Shanghai in order to arrive as soon as possible. Yesterday, the shipowner telegraphed that the ship would proceed directly to Shanghai from the Pacific Ocean without stopping en route. However, when the ship entered the Pacific Ocean, it encountered a hurricane. For the sake of safe navigation, the ship dropped anchor to avoid the storm. As a result, the arrival date in Shanghai was later than originally scheduled.

Loading Situation 123

This time, the American cotton purchased by our country is in the name of the national government as the consignee, and the bill of lading lists "Chinese Government Agency." The cotton shipped from the United States is done by a cotton purchasing organization established by our country in the United States, generally using the "Chinese-American Cotton Office for Economic Construction," with the following original English name: Order Reconstruction Finance Corporation Notify Chinese-American Cotton Syndicate.

Exact Date of Arrival in Shanghai 124

The ship is scheduled to arrive at Wusong on the 29th and can enter the port on the morning of the 30th. After arriving in Shanghai, the cotton is scheduled to berth and unload at the China Merchants' Wharf. If another ship is berthed at the wharf, it will be diverted to the Yangtze Wharf.

Fire Insurance Claims Association Demands Compensation from Jardine Matheson. Representatives Injured and Sent to Hospital for Treatment 133

Yesterday morning, the Fire Insurance Claims Association of the Zhabei Disaster Area publicly elected representatives to demand compensation from foreign firms such as Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire. As a result, they were driven away by the police, resulting in injuries to the representatives. The association has decided to continue to send representatives to proceed today, and the situation is likely to escalate.

Resolution to Demand Compensation 134

The household representatives' meeting believes that foreign firms such as Butterfield & Swire and Jardine Matheson have not yet expressed their views on the compensation issue and has resolved to go to demand compensation and ask for an effective response.

Election of Representatives 135

At 9:00 AM yesterday, the association publicly elected Fang Xi, Wang Zhixiang, members Wang Weigong, Xu Zaikang, Zheng Shaojin, Ma Rugen, and more than 360 household representatives, each wearing the Fire Insurance Claims Association badge, to depart from Baoshan Road. The association prepared food for the representatives when they departed. The order along the way was still good. They first went to the insurance department of Butterfield & Swire to demand compensation. Seven representatives, including Wang Zhixiang, went to the office. The firm said that the Westerner in charge of the insurance department was not there and asked them to contact them again later. The representatives then went to Jardine Matheson at No. 1 Guangdong Road.

Negotiations Fail 136

After 10:00 AM, the representatives went to Jardine Matheson and were also represented by seven people, including Wang, Ma, Zheng, and Xu, to negotiate with the insurance department of the firm. Wang and others submitted a written statement requesting an immediate response. Chen Songyuan, the comprador of Jardine Matheson, said that the matter involved the entire insurance industry and could not be expressed by one insurance firm alone. They must wait for the public to discuss and agree on a solution before they could discuss the solution with the policyholders. Therefore, he showed them his reply. The representatives, unable to get any substantive results, informed the household representatives who came with them. The crowd said that this matter could not be won with words, so fifty or so representatives, including men, women, old, and young, went to the outside of the writing room inside Jardine Matheson and sat down to wait for a solution.

Police Intervention 137

Jardine Matheson believed that dozens of male and female policyholders sitting on the second floor of the writing room were not elegant and hindered the flow of traffic, so they advised them to leave. The representatives refused to leave because they had not received a definite solution. Everyone also carried food, and there was a situation of sitting down outside. The firm immediately telegraphed the police to send officers to come. The officers arrived and persuaded them to leave peacefully. At 11:40 AM, a large team of Chinese and Western police officers rushed to the entrance of the second floor of Jardine Matheson and ordered everyone to leave. The representatives insisted on not agreeing. The Western police officers then ordered the Chinese police officers to forcibly drive them away. The Western police officers even dragged everyone down the stairs. During the commotion, four people were injured and sent to the hospital for treatment.

Representatives Injured 138

Policyholder representative Feng Qibiao, 22 years old, refused to leave when the Western police officers drove them away, and was dragged down from the second-floor stairs by a Western police officer and thrown to the lower level, seriously injured and unable to move. Four other representatives, Zhang Ziming, Cai Tongshan, Lu Yaoquan, and the woman Lin Gen, were either bumped or fell, and were also slightly injured. Each of the remaining people was dragged out by a Chinese police officer, causing the atmosphere on Guangdong Road Bund to suddenly become tense at around 10:00 AM. The injured were sent to the Second Branch of the Red Cross Hospital by the association's vehicles for treatment.

Emergency Meeting 139

After this incident occurred, about 300 household representatives who were waiting for news in the area of ​​Sichuan Road and Wuma Road were notified by Wang Zhixiang, the chairman of the association, and others to return to the association on Baoshan Road to hold an emergency meeting to discuss countermeasures and aftermath matters. For a time, the road was crowded. Jardine Matheson was protected by police officers to prevent a recurrence.

Agreed Solution 140

The reporter received the news and rushed to the association by car to investigate the situation. At that time, the meeting was being held. According to the spokesperson of the association, although the demand for compensation from Jardine Matheson today was frustrated, the association is determined to persevere and continue to fight. In addition to sending a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Concession, requesting that it uphold justice, and issuing a declaration seeking assistance from people in the community, they will decide to send representatives to the firm again tomorrow to negotiate and demand fire insurance compensation, until the goal is achieved. The injured members have been treated in the hospital, and the association is determined to send eight people tomorrow if four people are injured today. Therefore, it is expected that there may be another unfortunate incident today.

Submit Documents to the Party and Government 141

The document is submitted to the authorities requesting strict negotiations regarding the repeated assault on disaster victims by the police and to quickly determine a solution. The association is in the disaster area, and the fire insurance compensation in the disaster area has been negotiated for a long time, but there is no solution. The association continues to demand compensation in order to find a solution. However, since the compensation has continued, the insurance firms have not refused, and the insurance association has been unanimously entrusted to be responsible for the solution. However, in the process of demanding compensation, the police have repeatedly failed to understand the suffering of the disaster victims and have intervened arbitrarily, resulting in the incident that the previous compensation committee member Song Liangcai was violently beaten and injured by a Western police officer. The association has already reported this case. Unexpectedly, this morning, disaster victims went to Jardine Matheson on Wuma Road to demand compensation. Dozens of Chinese and Western detectives from the police station suddenly came and arbitrarily beat the disaster victims who were demanding compensation, which was extremely tyrannical and inhumane. Among those seriously injured were Feng Qibiao, Zhang Ziming, Cai Tongshan, Lin Gen, Chen Zhaotang, and others. They have been sent to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. However, the police are so disregarding of justice that the agency should negotiate with the authorities. However, the long-term dispute in this case is ultimately not a social blessing. Therefore, we respectfully ask the agency to review and approve and quickly determine a solution to protect the lives of the policyholders and maintain social security. We are extremely grateful. The submission is omitted below.

Ji Zejin Discusses the Stagnation of Chinese Tea Sales in Africa 142

The rise and fall of Chinese tea is closely related to the market, rescuing the African market and resisting the oppression of Japanese tea.

This is the most important and urgent task at present.

The sales situation of Chinese tea in Africa, according to Ji Zejin, the director of the Guidance Office of the International Trade Bureau, said yesterday:

Our Country's Tea Leaves 143

Each year, the amount sold to foreign countries is approximately 400,000 to 500,000 dan (a unit of weight). Green tea accounts for about three-quarters of the total. Among these, the export of Chun Mee and other varieties to French Africa reaches over 150,000 dan annually, with a total value exceeding ten million yuan. This trade has traditionally been

Handled by Foreign Merchants 144

for resale. Because there has been no direct relationship between tea merchants and African tea merchants, the mediation of foreign merchants has led to fraudulent practices such as coloring and adulteration.

Japanese Tea Competition 145

Japanese merchants have exploited this weakness in our country. In the past three years, they began competing with Chinese tea in the African market. Based on the principle of direct sales, they conducted vigorous propaganda to undermine Chinese tea, such as distributing various explanatory documents pointing out that Chinese tea contains toxic pigments, is adulterated, and is manufactured in a dirty and unsanitary manner. They boasted that Japanese green tea is purely the natural color of tea leaves, without any coloring or adulteration, and that it has been proven by famous medical professionals to contain large amounts of vitamins, and so on. Since our country has no direct agency stationed in Africa, we have been unable to refute these claims. Africans, failing to investigate, have taken our silence as tacit approval. Thus, they initially felt doubt, then trust. The sales of Japanese tea in Africa have increased rapidly. In three years, the import of Japanese tea into Africa has grown from six tons to two thousand tons, accounting for a quarter of the total tea imports. The urgency and danger facing the future of Chinese tea is evident.

Investigation by Authorities 146

The result of this aggressive dumping by Japanese tea and the real situation of coloring and adulteration of Chinese tea have attracted the attention of the French African colonial government. In order to understand the truth, they have sent a document to the French Indochina colonial government, specially dispatching tea expert Mr. Goubeaux to conduct an on-site investigation in both China and Japan. According to Mr. Goubeaux, his visit to Japan will focus on the organization of tea exporters and whether they have political backing. In China, he will focus on the cleanliness and hygiene of manufacturing procedures and the real situation of coloring and adulteration.

Relief Measures 147

Since our country's black tea market has been seized by Indian, Ceylonese, and Javanese black teas, only green tea exports remain considerable. Among green tea exports, only sales to Africa are the largest. Aside from Russia, the rest are all small and scattered. Therefore, the African market is the lifeline of our country's foreign-traded tea, and its rise and fall are most critical to our country's tea market. If Africa is lost, millions of tea farmers in our country will be forced into banditry. Therefore, saving the African tea market and resisting the oppression of Japanese tea is currently the most important and urgent task. After the African government amends the import regulations for colored tea this year, it will give Japanese tea more convenient sales opportunities. The tragic defeat of Chinese tea in the United States in the past is about to be repeated today. Although our country's government has regulations for tea inspection, because there is no direct sales organization, the regulations are ineffective. Even if they are勉强 enforced to comply with the import regulations of the African government, foreign merchants will further tighten tea market prices for profit, making it impossible for Chinese tea manufacturers and tea farmers to sustain themselves, leading to bankruptcy. Therefore, the government should send special personnel with all tea merchants on the sea to Africa to investigate the situation in detail, resist the propaganda of Japanese tea, and establish the first step of direct relationship between African tea merchants and sea tea merchants. At the same time, inland manufacturers should unite and collaborate. When the opportunity matures, take the second step of direct sales. And when the production and sales cooperatives of tea farmers in various places have a complete organization, take the third step, the final step of direct sales. Otherwise, Chinese tea will continue to be manipulated by foreign merchants, and in the not-too-distant future, it will disappear overseas.

Japanese Coal Dumping Causes Domestic Coal Prices to Fall 148

The Domestic Coal Relief Association is Discussing Relief Methods

According to coal market news, the price of domestic coal has fallen by about 30 cents per dan. The decline is more significant for coal from the Kailuan Mining Administration. The reason is the dumping of Japanese coal in China. The method of Japanese coal dumping is that purchasers do not need to pay cash. Therefore, a group of unscrupulous merchants are competing to purchase coal for profit and waiting for a shortage of coal on the market to raise prices. Domestic coal is more difficult to transport and is also squeezed by the dumping, causing sales prices to fall. The Domestic Coal Relief Association is currently discussing relief methods.
